<p><b>⇒ <u>19 more</u>:</b> Joy, Joy doth so arise - Lute score (tablature) • Crewell you pull away to soone - Lute score (tablature) • Ladie, those eies - Lute score (tablature) • Hould out my hart - Lute score (tablature) • God Morrow, Fayre Ladies - Lute score (tablature) • Whither awaie so fast - Lute score (tablature) • Blow, Shepherds, blow - Lute score (tablature) • Deep lamenting - Lute score (tablature) • Farewell disdainfull - Lute score (tablature) • O flye no - Lute score (tablature) • Thirsis - Lute score (tablature) • Now must I dye - Lute score (tablature) • Lady if I through griefe - Lute score (tablature) • Cease mine eyes - Lute score (tablature) • Doe you not know - Lute score (tablature) • Where art thou wanton - Lute score (tablature) • What ayles my darling - Lute score (tablature) • Say deere, will you not have me - Lute score (tablature) • Arise, get up my deere - Lute score (tablature)

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">A Collection of English Lute Trios
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Single-line Intabulations for 3 lutes (unison and a/g/D)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:H%C3%B6ger,_Anton" title="Category:Höger, Anton">Höger, Anton</a>
</td></tr>
<tr class="udelonly" data-display="table-row">
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Modern" title="Category:Modern">Modern</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Renaissance_style" title="Category:Renaissance style">Renaissance</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>3 lutes
</td></tr></table>
</div>
<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<ul><li>These "single-line" Intabulations are intended not only for training purposes for students (rhythm, listening sessions, interaction) but can be even small Encores in concerts. -
</li><li>Diese "einstimmigen" Intavolierungen sind nicht nur für Übungszwecke für Schüler gedacht, (Rhythmus, Hörtraining, Zusammenspiel) sondern können auch kleine Zugaben bei Konzerten sein.
</li></ul>
